## String References

- **16151**: @@
- **16624**: Read the manual? [Sure./No thanks.]
- **16625**: Mandragora Mania Madness is a game in which players battle by placing different colored game pieces on a 4x4 playing area.
- **16626**: You use the white pieces (mandragoras), while your opponent uses the black pieces (corrigans).
- **16627**: The player to go first is determined randomly when the game begins. You will be able to adjust these settings yourself from the second game onward.
- **16628**: The first player to place four pieces so they align in a row will be declared the winner.
- **16629**: However, you will automatically be disqualified if you ever place three of your pieces in a row, so be mindful of your moves at all times.
- **16630**: Note that if you place your game pieces so that you have both three and four pieces in a row, the row with four pieces will take precedence and you will win the game.
- **16631**: If you place a game piece on either side of your opponent's piece, you will convert it into one of your pieces.
- **16632**: You can play anywhere from three to five games, and the first player to win three games is the winner.
- **16633**: Now, for an explanation on points.
- **16634**: You receive points after the completion of each game. The points are tallied using units known as mandy.
- **16635**: If you win the game, you will receive a number of points equal to the number of game pieces you have on the board. In the example shown, you will earn 8 mandy.
- **16636**: Even if you lose the game, you will receive a number of points equal to half the number of your game pieces on the board (rounded off to avoid fractions).
- **16637**: The first player to win three games gets to keep all of the points they have earned, although you won't get any points if you quit partway.
- **16638**: Occasionally, you might get to play a bonus game, where your pieces are pink (adenium) or feature a watermelon pattern (citrullus).
- **16639**: They are worth $0x and $1x the points, respectively, giving you the chance to quickly score a large number of points.
- **16640**: The key to victory is to not just try and place four pieces in a row, but to position your pieces in a way that forces your opponent to place three pieces in a row.

#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x19A4 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()

    → "@@"

  8: 0x19BB [0x5C] MUSIC_CONTROL: Set Idle (Night) music to song 64*
```
